Our website uses cookies, which could include also third party cookies, to send advertising that is relevant to you.</p><p><strong><em>Are all cookies the same?</em></strong><br>Cookie can be classified as it follows.<br><em>Session cookies. </em>These cookies are automatically erased when you close your browser.<br><em>Persistent cookies.</em> These cookies remain on your device until they expire (in terms of minutes, days or years since the cookie creation/update).<br><em>Third-Party cookies. </em> These cookies are stored on behalf of third parties.<br>Cookies can be managed and deleted by setting your browser.
